GCIG PHYAG GNYIS PA ZHIG KRONG NGE 'DUG PA GZIGS TE BLA MAR ZHUS
PAS KHYOD KYIS DPAL TSAN PO'I GRUB PA THOB PAR 'DUG PAS 'U CAG
RNAMS 'DANGS GSUNGS NAS SHANGS KYI SGRUB KHAR GDONG DU PHEBS, DER

LHA KHANG BRTZIG PAR THAG BCAD NAS SA 'DUL MDZAD PAS BLA MA DPAL
CHEN DU MTHONG BA MANG PO BYUNG, GRVA PA KUN GYIS RDO RJE BSKYAL
NAS ZUR CHUNG PAS GYAD RDO ZHIG BZHAG YONG GLENGS PAS MANG MA TSA
BA LA SONG SHUL BDE GSHEGS RGYA BOS PHA BOD BSGUL MI THUB PA DE

PHYOGS; BZHE MTSAMS BZHIR BZHAG PAS GZHAN RNAMS CHAGS SDANG DANG
BRAL TE GUS PAR GYUR, 'OG KHANG GI KA BA 'KHYOG PO BZHI YANG MDA'
LTAR BSRANGS, LHA RJES GNUBS NAM MKHA'I SNYING PO'I LUNG BSTAN
BZHIN DPAL CHEN PO'I SKU BZHENG BA'I STA GON GYI TSE

TING NGE 'DZIN GYIS BKUG PAS LHA BZON KHAS PA 'DRA CHOS ZHU BAR
'ONGS PA YIN ZER 'BYOR BAR CHOS CI 'DOD YONG BAS DUS KYI SNYIGS
MAR DAG PHYOGS RNAMS 'DUL BA'I DPAL CHEN PO'I SKU ZHIG 'GRUB NA
'GRO DON CHE BAS GROGS GYIS GSUNG BA BZHIN KHAS BLANGS,

DAM RDZAS DANG SA SNA RDO SNA SOGS SKU RGYU DANG BSRES PA'I THOG
TSAD CIG BZHENG BA'I ZHAL BKOD MDZAD, BZO GANG LEGS BYAS KYANG
ZHAL GZIGS DANG MA MTHUN PAS SANG NGA LA BLTAS NAS BZHINGS NA
YONG BAS SHOG GSUNGS DE NYIN ZUR CHUNG BA DANG BZO PO SOGS 'DUS

PAR BLA MA DPAL CHEN PHYAG GNYIS PA, ZHABS G-YAS DUG PA LUNG GI
BRAG GDOR DANG, G-YON BTZAD PO PUR KHANG ZHES PA'I RI RTZER BZHAG
PAS BZO PO RNAMS DE ZHIG DRAN MED DU SONG, DRAN GSOS NAS SKU'I
LTE BA MAN CHAD CAM LAS MI DRAN PA 'DUG DA ZHAL GSUM

NGA NYID LTA BU'I

GNAS MNGA' GSOL GYI CHAS DGON PAR ZUR CHUNG BAS 'OG GDONG BRAG GI

'DRA YANG LOG RTOG GI ZING ZING PO KHO NAR GYUR PAR MTHONG BAS

'BRI GUNG ZHABS

ZHIG LHA SA DANG 'BRAS SPUNGS SU 'ONGS PA'I GA RE 'BROM

@105B KHA MA ZHUGS PA'I KHUNGS BTZUN PA AE NAS RIGS 'DZIN CHOS
DBANG KUN BZANG LA GSAN TE GUNG THANG DU PHEBS ZLA SHAS BZHUGS
PAR BKA' BRGYAD BDE 'DUS, 'JAM DPAL RDZOGS CHEN SOGS MTHA' YAS PA
GSAN, RIN PO CHE CHOS SDINGS PA DANG GRUB CHEN KARMA GSANG SNGAGS
GNYIS

LA RIGS 'DZIN SROG SGRUB KYI DBANG LUNG GSAN ZHING GRUB CHEN
GSANG SNGAGS PAR RDZOGS PA CHEN PO SANGS RGYAS MNYAM SPYOR GYI
LUNG SOGS CHOS BKA' CI RIS GSAN, GAR PAR DBYAR MJAL LA PHEBS PA'I
NUB 'OD GSAL DU JO BO SH'AKYA MU NE'I SKU MDUN DU BLA MA BLA GOS
THAR SOR BZHES

PA'I DBU DKAR BA ZHIG LA MI MANG POS GUS 'DUD BYAD 'DUG PA SU YIN
DRI BA GNANG PAR BKA' GDAMS KYI DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN BYA 'CHAD KA
BA YIN ZER, DES RJE NYID LA PHYAG MDZAD PA MYUNG BA SANG NYIN
GSANG PHU RNAM RGYAL GSER BKANG PA'I DRUNG CHEN DKON COG DPAL
'BYOR GUNG THANG

GSAN RES MDZAD, 'JAM DBYANGS BLA MA DKON COG CHOS 'PHEL DAG ZHING
DU GSHEGS RJES GRUNG [?] CHEN 'DI LAS MKHAS BTZUN BZANG BA ZHIG
GSANG SNE'U THOG PHYOGS SU MA BYUNG BAR MA ZAD KHYAD PAR RDZOGS
PA CHEN PO DANG GSUNG

NGAG LAM 'BRAS GNYIS KA LA PHUL DU PHYIN ZHING BYANG CHUB KYI
SEMS LA MNGA' 'BYOR BAS 'CHAD KA BA YE SHES RDO RJE'I RNAM SPRUL
DU THE MI TSOM PAR GNANG, NGED GTZANG NAS 'KHOR BA DANG BSTUN
ZHAG SHAS RJE NYID 'BRAS SPUNGS SU BZHUGS PA'I GZHIS KA SHAR LAGS
AA GUR GYIS ZHING BKOD KHA

BAR BRIS PA'I ZHAL BKOD DANG SHOG DPE GNANG, BYAD PA RIGS 'DZIN
CHEN PO'I RNAM THAR 'DRI DGOS TSUL PHEBS PA BZHIN NYER BA SNGOGS
BYAS, ZLA BA BCU GCIG PA'I NANG DU RJE BLA MA 'BRAS SPUNGS SU
GDAN DRANGS DGONGS 'DUS KYI DBANG CHEN DBANG PHRAN GYIS GTZOS
PA'I CHOS BKA' MANG DU

*, ,RTAG 'BAR BA'I, ,BKRA SHIS DPAL GYIS 'JIG RTEN YONGS KHYAB
SHOG ,CES DUS GSUM RGYAL BA THAMS CAD KYI MKHYEN BRTZE NUS PA'I
BDAG NYID KHYAB BDAG RDO RJE SEMS DNGOS

ZUR THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA CHOS DBYINGS RANG GROL GYI RNAM THAR THEG
MCHOG BSTAN PA'I SHING RTA ZHES PA 'DI NI RANG NYID LA BRI 'DUN
SNGA MO NAS YOD PA DANG, NYE CHAR RJE BTZUN BLA MA MCHOG GI THUGS
SRAS DAM PA RIGS

'DZIN SPRUL PA'I SKU MCHOG BLO BZANG PADMA 'PHRIN LAS THEG MCHOG
DBANG GI RGYAL PO YONGS 'DU'I SDE'I GSUNG GIS BSKUL ZHING GZHAN
YANG GZHIS KA SHAR PA LAGS AA GUR SPUN NGAG DBANG 'PHRIN LAS, MES

KYI SNGAGS 'CHANG KHRO RGYAL DPAL MGON SOGS DON GNYER CAN DU MAS
BSKUL BA LA BRTEN NAS BLA MA'I BKA' 'BANGS ZA HOR GYI SNGAGS
SMYON GANG SHAR RANG GROL GYIS ME 'BRUG HOR ZLA BRGYAD PA'I DKAR
CHA'I BZANG

BGYIS PA PHYOGS DUS KUN TU DGE ZHING BKRA SHIS PAR GYUR CIG,
